# Beta Agents Endpoints

(beta) Agents API

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List agent entities._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve a list of agent entities sorted by creation time.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_code-samples_typescript">

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.list({});

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.list(page=0, page_size=20)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_code-samples_curl"

cURL

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents \

```

</SectionContent>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_responses_200_application-json_agent_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"
  id="Agent_completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format_ResponseFormat"

  parentId="Agent_completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format"

  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandableBreakoutTitle slot="title">

#### ResponseFormat \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list_responses_200_application-json_agent_completion_args_completionargs_response_format_responseformat\}

</ExpandableBreakoutTitle>

<ExpandableBreakoutDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandableBreakoutDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create a agent that can be used within a conversation._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a new agent giving it instructions, tools, description. The agent is then available to be used as a regular assistant in a conversation or as part of an agent pool from which it can be used.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.create({
    model: "LeBaron",
    name: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.create(model="LeBaron", name="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "model": "ipsum eiusmod",
  "name": "consequat do"
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_request_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"

  expandByDefault={false}
>

#### ResponseFormat \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_request_completion_args_completionargs_response_format_responseformat\}

</ExpandableBreakoutTitle>

<ExpandableBreakoutDescription slot="description">

When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandableBreakoutDescription>

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Retrieve an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Given an agent retrieve an agent entity with its attributes.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_typescript">

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.get({
    agentId: "<id>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.get(agent_id="<id>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents/{agent_id} \
 -X GET \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<ExpandableProperty

  headingId="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format"
  parentId="completion_args_CompletionArgs"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"ResponseFormat","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format_responseformat\">ResponseFormat</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"
  id="completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format_ResponseFormat"
  headingId="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format_responseformat"
  parentId="completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format"
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandableBreakoutTitle slot="title">

#### ResponseFormat \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format_responseformat\}

</ExpandableBreakoutTitle>

<ExpandableBreakoutDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandableBreakoutDescription>

<ExpandableBreakoutProperties slot="properties">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update an agent attributes and create a new version.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.update({
    agentId: "<id>",
    agentUpdateRequest: {},
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.update(agent_id="<id>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_request_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. <ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"
  id="completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format_ResponseFormat"

  parentId="completion_args_CompletionArgs_response_format"

  expandByDefault={false}
>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\}/version \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent version._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Switch the version of an agent.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.updateVersion({
    agentId: "<id>",
    version: 157995,
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.update_version(agent_id="<id>", version=157995)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_code-samples_curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents/{agent_id}/version \
 -X PATCH \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### response_format \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version_responses_200_application-json_completion_args_completionargs_response_format\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specify the format that the model must output. By default it will use `\{ "type": "text" \}`. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_schema" \}` enables JSON schema mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON and follows the schema you provide.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyBreakouts slot="breakouts">
